Y, si le gusta, no olvide valorarnos con 5 estrellas.\r\n\r\n− Qué es una VPN\r\nVPN son las iniciales de Virtual Private Network (red privada virtual). Al conectarse a un servidor VPN a través del Proxy de la VPN de Hotspot Shield, por ejemplo, se establece una conexión segura y cifrada con un servidor en otro país. El proceso de cifrado impide que los datos se filtren o bloqueen. \r\n\r\n− Por qué usar una VPN\r\nCon una VPN, no solo puede desbloquear servicios censurados o con restricciones geográficas, como Facebook, Pandora y Youtube, sino que, además, podrá navegar por Internet de forma anónima y con más privacidad y seguridad.\r\n\r\n- VPN frente a proxy\r\nTanto una VPN como un proxy pueden camuflar su identidad cambiando la ruta del tráfico de Internet y la IP. Sin embargo, un servidor proxy se basa por completo en el navegador y podría no ser compatible con determinadas páginas web que usan tecnología no basada en navegador. Por el contrario, un servicio de VPN cifra todo el tráfico y funciona con servicios basados en Internet. En resumen, una VPN proporciona más libertad, privacidad y seguridad al navegar por Internet.\r\n\r\n− ¿Por qué elegir la VPN de Hotspot Shield?\r\nLa VPN de Hotspot Shield es la marca de VPN de mayor confianza y ofrece un rendimiento óptimo en cuanto a velocidad, estabilidad y seguridad. In an entirely frozen world, people develop steam-powered technology to oppose the overwhelming cold. The city’s ruler has to manage both the citizens and the infrastructure they live in. The leader’s tactical skills face challenges that will frequently question morality and the basic foundations of what we consider organized society. Optimization and resource management often clash with empathy and thoughtful decision-making. While city and society management will consume most of the ruler’s time, at some point exploration of the outside world is necessary to understand its history and present state.\r\n\r\nWhat decisions will you make to ensure the survival of your society? What will you do when pushed to the limit? And...\r\n\r\n...who will you become in the process?\r\n\r\nMAKE THE LAW\r\nSociety is a group of people who abide by the same rules and share similar beliefs. Establish laws that regulate the existence of your growing society. Decide on their working routine, healthcare, food provision and other crucial aspects of everyday life. Maintain their hope and contentment – the moral condition of your society is as important as securing the basic means to keep them fed and safe.\r\n\r\nWEIGH UP YOUR CHOICES\r\nSome of your decisions will seem small – like deciding the fate of a troubled citizen or meeting the demands of a newborn faction – but be aware that the sum of your doings can lead to unexpected results. Your people put their faith in you, but their devotion is not limitless. Leadership can be a burden.\r\n\r\nDEVELOP NEW TECHNOLOGIES\r\nSurvival demands progress. Providing a highly advanced infrastructure with self-powered automatons, airships and other technical wonders is difficult, but achievable.
